3a2(5): dod pa zhig gda' 'o// zhabs kyi 'og nas pad ma dgu brtsigs pa'i gdan bting ba zhig gda' 'o// de la yab yum blon po 'khor dang bcas pa thams cad/ shin tu ngo mtshar skyes 
3a3(5): te/ lha'i ltas mkhan la dres/ lha'i sras po 'd kyi khe' chung bya ba 'di/ dang por yang dgo des che zhing na tshul bzang pa/ g.sung dug bon la yid gzhung la/ bar du 'ang lha yi glu gar 
3a4(5): dang rtsi 'dol la mi byin par nyi shel 'cher ba'i phug na dgongs pa byed/ tha mar kyang shin tu ngo mtshar che ba 'di lta bu'i rtags dang ldan pa 'di/ ji ltar zhig lags zhes zhus pas/ 
3a5(5): lha'i lhas mkhan gyis gsungs pa/ 'di ni mae dang lha'i sras lta bur me 'dug ste/ dus gsum gyi bde bar ghegs pa rnams kyi byin rlabs/ ston pa gnhen lha 'di dkar gyi sprul pa 
3a6(5): cig gda' 'o// 'di yi spyi bo'i gtsug na rin po che 'di 'bar ba'i stengs na/ a dkar po chu shel gyi mdog lta bu gnas pa ni/ khyab bdal mi g.yo bon gyi sku dang ldan zhing / 
3b1(5): rang bzhin spros bral gyi don khong du chud nas/ rig pa ye shes kyi rtsal/ sku dang yi shes sna tshogs su 'char ba'i rtags yin/ zhal gyi ldags las pad ma gi sar mdzes pa'i me / 
3b2(5): tog kha daog legs zhing dbyibs tdug par gnas pa ni/ longs spyod s+dzogs pa'i sku mtshan dang dpe byad du ldan zhing / gsung tshangs pa'i sgra dbyangs kyi/ bon 'dul ngag bden pa ston 
3b3(5): pa'i rtags yin/ thugs las gser gyi nyi ma stong phrag grangs med pa 'phro ba ni/ lha ya bu las spul pa'i sku bye ba phrag brgya grangs med par byung nas/ sems can gyi kha lo 
3b4(5): gyen du 'dren cing / 'gro drug thugs rjes 'dzin pa'i rtags yin/ sku yi lte ba las rin po zur brgyad pa mdzes shing brjod pa rin po che'i shu gur dod pa na/ lha spyod dgongs pa'i 
3b5(5): yon tan dpag tu med pa dang ldan zhing 'du ma byas kyi yon tan chen pos/ ma rig pa'i mun pa sangs par byed pa'i rtags yin/ zhabs kyi 'og nas pad ma dgu brtsigs kyi gdan / 
3b6(5): bting ba ni/ khams gsum 'khor ba dong nas sugs zhing / theg pa rim pa dgus 'gro ba 'dren pa'i rtags yin/ zhes gsungs pas/ yab yum blon po 'khor dang bcas pa rnams 
4a1(5): kyang / shin du rje 'du yern zhi grung pa'i tshul dng / brtse ba'i sams kyi sntor badang lha byag byedo// phyogs bco'i br gshegs lt dgons 'das pa'i rgyud la'o/ 
4a2(5): lo rgyus gleng gzhi' le'u ste dang po'o// de nas lha'i sras po 'od kyi khye'u chung zhes bya ba d/ dgongs pa bon nyid ngang las bzhengs te/ lha dang mi las sogs pa'i 'gro ba log par rtogs 
4a3(5): pa/ phyen ci log tu kha brgyud cing / 'khor bar 'khyams pa rnams bu gcig pa la mas gdung pa lthar/ shin tu brtse zhing snying brtse ba'i sems skyes te/ yi dam gyi lha gnhen lha 
4a4(5): 'od dkar la sogs pa'i/ phyogs bcu'i bder gshegs thams cad la 'di skad ces bskul lo// kye ma phyogs bcu'i bder gshegs rnams/ yon tan gter ldan gsang ba'i 
4a5(5): mdzod/ thugs rje'i chu bo rgyun ma 'chad/ kun grol rnam dag de la gtod/ bdag la gsan zhing dgongs su gsol/ ma rig 'khor ba'i sems can rnams/ b prug ma yis 
4a6(5): ber ba ltar/ ltos gzhi med pa snying ro rje/ khams gsum kha 'khor rgyu drug lus len zhing / phyi nang sdug bsngal mi grol yi re mug/ byas pa mi zin las la zad pa med/ rnam 
4b1(5): rtog dra ba mi pril bhang re chad/ 'gro ba lha dang ma ni shes pa zhing / dbang po yul la yengs pa'i gzung 'dzin gyis/ thar lam mi thob sdug bsngal zad dus med/ long ba'i 'gros

5a1(5): y/ par dga' ba'i 'jig rten po brang yongs su dag pa'i zhing khams na/ kun tu bzang po ma nub pa'i rtags can gyis 'di skad ces gsungs so// rang 'byung ye shes 'du ma / 
5a2(5): byas/ kun khyab nam mkha' lta bu la/ sna tshogs 'byung ba rig pa'i gting / gting dpag bcad dka' rgya mtsho'i gling / dri med rang shar mtha' dang bral/ sems nyid kun tu bzang po /

5b1(5): g.yung dung can gyis/ 'di skad ces gsungs so// khyung chen gshig s+dzogs bar snang mkha' la lding / thams cad khobs chub gang la nyam mi nga/ kun gsal rning ldan stong gsum /

6a1(5): 'bhrul pa'i khro skur rang las me/ blo bnag rgom pa'grol 'dod pa/ 'dzin pas byang tsher thags du gu/ tcon nyid gzug ma'i dgongs pa la/ rang byung ye zhes /

6a3(5): mchong / nyamsg tshul 'chos bag tsha' rnam rtog med/ de bzhin rig pa'i snying po byang chub sems/ yon tan rtsal s+dzogs nyon mongs zil gyis gnon/ sgros 'dog skur 'dabs 
6a4(5): gang gis nyam nga med/ bsam med ting 'dzin rkyen dang bral/ ma g.yos ma bcos nyid du bde/ snang ba med pa'i bon nyid ni/ ma brtsal dang po nyid du bde/ brjod du med pa'i bon nyid la/
